general 2022-04-29 13:30:44 So, if you use a basic motor they are able to create a large amount of torque, on an irl heli, this is controlled with a tail rotor that is hooked directly into the driveshaft so that the rotor and tail rotor are always perfectly counteracting eachother. Now there's your first problem, since you would have to control the pitch of the blades with control surfaces, it will suddenly create a large amount of resistance, thus leading your tail rotor to not be sufficient enough, and makes it very unstable and hard to control, fake rotors and hover rotors make it much more controlae and at that point, function takes priority over realism. Tldr, basic motors are hard to control and hover rotors perform better, and most times, look better than basic motors
